    case Node(_, l, _, r) =>
      (blackBalanced(l) && blackBalanced(r) && (blackHeight(l) == blackHeight(r)))
    case _ =>
      true
  })}

    case Empty() =>
      true
    case Node(Black(), l, _, r) =>

    case Node(Red(), l, _, r) =>

    case _ =>

  case class Red() extends Color

  sealed abstract class Color

  def blackBalanced(t : Tree) : Boolean = {(t match {
    case Node(_, l, _, r) =>
      (blackBalanced(l) && blackBalanced(r) && (blackHeight(l) == blackHeight(r)))
    case _ =>
      true
  })}

  })}
